< text>
I have taken all of my cats and dogs to VMC for the past 17 years or so. Many years before that, when I was a teenager, Dr. Holstein would come to our small ranch to treat our goats. So he's been doing this for a long time. Everyone in the VMC office is so friendly and helpful. The veterinarians are very caring, knowledgeable, thorough, and take the time to explain what is going on with your pet in easy to understand terms. They tell you all of your options, tell you what they recommend, and then let you make the call. Over the years, I have had a number of pets enter the ends of their lives and have to be put to sleep. Dr. Klintworth has been there for my pets and for me through them all. She always brings in blankets to make my pet comfortable, explains what she is going to do, explains what will happen with my pet, and gives me the time I need with my pet both before and after. She is always so compassionate and, she too, loves on my pet before and after. On one occasion, when my children were young, they went with me. Dr. Klintworth explained everything to them, answered all of their questions, and helped comfort them before and after. I can't say enough good things about VMC and I highly recommend them. They are the best of the best.< /text>

< text>
Veterinary Medical Center is a blessing to my family. They have competitive rates and we are grateful that their cost is fair. They have even worked with us in a few situations in meeting our needs. They are gracious and forgiving when we forget to show up for an appointment (it only happened once, yikes) and provide excellent and thorough care to all of our farm critters. The vets there have gone above and beyond to save the life of our goat and our cat. While in their care I was allowed to visit my cat on my schedule (provided there was someone in the facility) and they never mocked my crazy nerves any time a pet is sick. I can't recommend them enough. On a practical note : the other vet offices in town care for house cats and dogs, the vets in this office have a background in large animal/ranch care. So, if your pet has caught something from the great outdoors they will be more likely to diagnose it here as I bet they are more familiar with the dangers of our local surroundings. I definitely recommend giving them a chance.</text>

< Review>
New place that just recently opened up on the Main Street pedestrian promenade. The food is a great addition to the downtown eateries. If the hours posted are correct, this establishment is open 24 hours.

We tried the fried rice and the ramen dishes. Both were really great tasting. The food quality is good and so odd the price. The dining seating area leaves allot to be desired. The offer steel benches which are not the most comfortable and the soda fountain drinks are mostly cream soda flavors.</Review>

< Text>
Been hitting a lot of ramen places lately and this is one of, if not the best. My only gripe is it's kind of a build you're own bowl, which is fine in itself, but the starting price point is what a normal (already loaded) bowl would cost then by the time you load it up, you're getting into the $15 - $20 a bowl range. So it's a bit pricey, but it's really tasty. So it's worth the once in a while splurge.</Text>

< Text>
I have a little Miniture Poodle mix with severe anxiety. Everything from separation anxiety to just anxiety in general. After I rescued her I worked a lot with her anxiety and though she improved a lot, I thought grooming may be out of the picture for a while. But I tested my chances with All-Paws and I'm so happy I did. Her first appointment she was very nervous shaking and growling, I was surprised I didnt get a call to go pick her up because they couldn't get her under control. - I just dropped her off for her 3rd appointment this morning, and she ran up to the door excited to be there. I couldn't believe it. This is definitely our grooming spot now! I dont know what they are doing in there that is working so well for my dog, but I couldnt be more appreciative of their patience and hard work. Thank you All-Paws! This is one of the few places where $15 a cocktail is absolutely worth it. Read through the drink menu - almost all of the drinks have flavor combinations that you would have never thought of and every single drink is delicious. The food is great too - definitely not an afterthought like many bars in the covid era.

The seating is well spaced out for social distancing and the wait staff is courteous and quick.

Well worth the premium price tag.< /text>

112623089326463590809<//userid>
<username>Sean Miller< /username><Time>1576384035969< /Time><Rating>5</Rating>< text>
Be sure to give this place a visit in the holiday season when it decks out to become "Miracle", a local favorite Yuletide "pop-up" bar! In a city somewhat starved of classic holiday activities & venues (aside from the Christmas tree & lit up palm trees in Union square, there is really not much to write home about on the Holiday spirit front), this bar would probably be among my top recommendations for those looking to get into the Christmas spirit. There is not much seating, it gets crowded very early, and drinks are on the expensive side to say the least ($16-20 cocktails! - but rest assured, most are fantastic, such as the popular Buddy's nog). Pro tip: come early (on weeknights around 4pm if you can, 5pm latest) and there will likely be no line + still a couple seats available.< /text>

<userid>100557202621809664171< /userid><user_name>Greg Bybee</user_name><time>1557629758305< /time><Rate>2< /Rate>< text>
Fantastic original cocktails with inventive ingredients and interesting presentation. I have always enjoyed my drinks at PCH.  But customer service is awful, and the venue is too small.

Two major problems:
1 - It's too small and crowded. This is partly due to popularity, but also due to a really small venue with bad layout.  The bar is right in the front, and most of the seating is in the back, so there's a chokepoint - it's very hard to get past the bar to the back. They also don't have near enough seating, and have wasted a lot of space with hallways that can't really be used to stand.

2 - They rush you out.  I was there on a date recently and they rushed us out after our second drink.  We arrived at 8:15 on Friday and got our first drinks around 8:30.  We ordered a second round of drinks around 9-9:15.  Around 9:45 as we were finishing those drinks, the server asked if we wanted another and we said "we're good right now."  We didn't necessarily mean we were done, just taking a break.  The server brought us the check.We let it sit there, since we weren't ready to go and might even want another drink. About 5-10 minutes later, the server came to ask us to pay so he could give the seat to another group.  WTF?  I said we were still chatting and might drink more, to give us a bit.  5 minutes later, another person, presumably a manager, came to ask us to leave.  Seriously?  We spent $70 on four drinks and they kicked us out less than 15 minutes after we finished the last drink.

I understand that a busy bar doesn't want people hanging around for a long time if they aren't drinking, but this was something else - they literally asked us to leave as soon as we finished our drinks and passed on the next round.  I couldn't believe it, especially from one of my favorite cocktails bars in SF.<//text>

<Response>None< /Response>< Review>
"Your friendly neighborhood bar" is what how the website greets you. An understatement.

From the welcoming and accommodating service (bring your own food, or order from Hogwash next door) to the exquisite, ever-changing cocktail menu, this place is the new hot spot in San Francisco.

The drinks are creative and fairly priced ($12-$15). My favorites: the spicy Swizzle My Nizzle (Olmeca Altos Blanco Tequila, passion fruit, vanilla, lime, habanero bitters, $13) and the amazingly fresh Ko'olina Swizzle (Banks 7 Rum, Banks 5 Rum, banana, orgeat, pineapple, bitters, $13). I do like my drinks on the sweeter side, but there are plenty of other options on the menu.

Cocktail lovers stop by - this is a great spot.<//Review>
